###########################
# Ireland Events
###########################

add_namespace = ire
add_namespace = irelandflavour

#########################################################
### Mobilize Event (from focus)
#########################################################

country_event = {
	id = ire.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.1" }
	title = ire.1.t
	desc = ire.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_army_marching

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_manpower = -36000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A full fighting company of eight divisions will be mobilized throughout the nation."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_FULL
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_manpower = -18000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A half-strength fighting company of four divisions will be mobilized throughout the nation."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_HALF
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_manpower = -9000
		custom_effect_tooltip = "A reserve infantry company of two divisions will be mobilized in Dublin and Belfast."
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				load_oob = IRE_MOBILIZE_WEAK
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ire.530
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.530" }
	title = ire.530.t
	desc = ire.530.d

		IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.530.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
}

# Hidden event to start tension mechanics
country_event = {
	id = ire.3000
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.3000" }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		set_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
		country_event = { id = ire.3 days = 30 }
	}
}
# Hidden event to fire tension events
country_event = {
	id = ire.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.3000" }
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = ire.3 days = 20 random_days = 80 }
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event
		country_event = ire.43
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_factory_clash_event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event
		country_event = ire.44
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = IRE_UVF_shooting_event
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_antrim_concert_shooting_event }
		}

			factor = 5

				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}

			}

	}

	option = {

			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_grand_opera_house_fire_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_grand_opera_house_fire_event
		country_event = ire.50
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_bank_robbery_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_bank_robbery_event
		country_event = ire.51
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 2 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_dublin_bombing_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_dublin_bombing_event

	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_pushing_for_independence_event }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_pushing_for_independence_event
		country_event = ire.58
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain }
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }
		set_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
		country_event = ire.36
	}

	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_tensions > 19 }
			check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation > 3 }
			owns_state = 119
			controls_all_owned_states = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = IRE_unionist_protest_event_chain
				
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = IRE_ulster_conflict
		country_event = ire.133 #Civil War
	}

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.625
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { ire_unionist_escalation = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ire.36
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.36" }
	title = ire.36.t
	desc = ire.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.36.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				country_event = {
					id = ire.63
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.36.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			IRE = {
				country_event = {
					id = ire.37
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Deploying Soldiers

country_event = {
	id = ire.39
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.39" }
	title = ire.39.t
	desc = ire.39.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_deploy_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.39.a
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Eoin_O'Duffy_dead }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		set_country_flag = ire_barry_in_charge
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.39.b
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		set_country_flag = ire_mulcahy_in_charge
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.39.c
		trigger = {
			IRE_has_michael_collins = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		set_country_flag = ire_lynch_in_charge
	}

	option = {

# Unionist Protest March 3

country_event = {
	id = ire.38
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.38" }
	title = ire.38.t

	desc = {

country_event = { #Unionist Uprising
	id = ire.133
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.133" }
	title = ire.133.t
	desc = ire.133.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_civil_war

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 8926 }
				set_nationality = ULS
				set_leader_portrait = GFX_Portrait_Ulster_James_Steele
			}
			news_event = { id = northernireland.1690 }
			ULS = {
				add_state_core = 119 #Ulster
				transfer_state = 119
				transfer_technology = yes
				add_ideas = {
					ULS_catholics
					partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
				division_template = {
					name = "Ulster Volunteers"
					division_names_group = ULS_MIL_01
					regiments = {
						militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
						militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
						militia = { x = 3 y = 0 }
					}
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_no_surrender days = 365 }
				unlock_national_focus = ULS_for_god_and_ulster
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = ULS_alliance_with_entente }
			}
			119 = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ally_with = ROOT
							has_military_access_to = ROOT
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Ulster Volunteers\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = ULS
					count = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_KILLUVF }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED4 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_REOCCBF }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED3 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_RTUG }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED2 days = 365 }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = IRE_REPRESS }
				ULS = {
					add_timed_idea = { idea = ULS_WEAKENED1 days = 365 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = ire.133.a
		add_political_power = -100
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ULS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		activate_mission = IRE_take_belfast
	}
	option = {
		name = ire.133.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_political_power = -100
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ULS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		activate_mission = IRE_take_belfast
		ULS = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}
}

# Yearly Immigration Waves
# Three 'levels' deciding population income. Low world tension, high world tension, and Ireland's war status (being at war dramatically reduces immigration for obvious reasons)

country_event = {
	id = ire.98
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.98 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = ire.98.t
	#LWT
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			threat < 0.5
		}
	}
	#HWT
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d2
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			threat > 0.5
		}
	}
	#IW
	desc = {
		text = ire.98.d3
		trigger = {
			has_war = yes
		}
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_immigration

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = IRE_EIE
		check_variable = { IRE_immigration_year < global.year } #to avoid firing multiple times per year
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = { IRE_immigration_year = global.year }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ire.98 days = 365 }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.98.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
				119 = { add_manpower = 7233 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 5541 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 3603 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 4921 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
				119 = { add_manpower = 3465 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 2478 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 4532 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 3105 }
			}
			else = {
				119 = { add_manpower = 3250 }
				134 = { add_manpower = 198 }
				135 = { add_manpower = 1732 }
				113 = { add_manpower = 4070 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { threat > 0.5 }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 64500 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 25402 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 21510 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 41705 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 17150 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 16623 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 14291 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 13032 }
				}
				else = {
					119 = { add_manpower = 9412 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 9420 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 8953 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 11550 }
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 2 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 14335 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 16205 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 15503 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 18023 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = { flag = IRE_immigration value = 1 } }
					119 = { add_manpower = 8232 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 7405 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 7721 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 8712 }
				}
				else = {
					119 = { add_manpower = 3456 }
					134 = { add_manpower = 4321 }
					135 = { add_manpower = 3621 }
					113 = { add_manpower = 5251 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ire.14
	immediate = {

			}

				days = 100
				random_days = 20
			}
		}
	}

	desc = ire.14.d

		IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
		date < 1938.1.1
		NOT = {	has_country_flag = IRE_1937_elections }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { # Work with SF
		name = ire.254.a
		
		custom_effect_tooltip = marlib_will_join_coalition_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_FG_SocDem
		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				name = IRE_social_democrat_party
				long_name = IRE_social_democrat_party_long
				ideology = market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_FG_pop = party_popularity@market_liberal
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_SF_pop = party_popularity@social_democrat
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_FG_pop
				value = current_SF_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = current_FG_pop
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Michael Collins"
				desc = "POLITICS_MICHAEL_COLLINS_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_Michael_Collins.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = { IRE_Waining_Personality }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = IRE_Old_Dog_New_Tricks
				}
				remove_country_leader_trait = IRE_Waining_Personality
				add_country_leader_trait = IRE_Big_Fellow
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire.318
				days = 76
			}
			add_marlib_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = ire.18
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.18" }
	title = ire.18.t
	desc = ire.18.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dail_meeting
	
	trigger = {
		IRE_has_michael_collins = no
		IRE_has_monarchy = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_labour_elections }
		has_country_flag = IRE_1937_elections
		NOT = {	has_country_flag = IRE_1942_Election_Held }
		
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_labour_occupies_socdem_slot }
		}

			text = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat

					election_frequency = 60
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}

		}

				election_frequency = 60
			}

		}

				add_ideas = {

country_event = {

	desc = ire.22.d

	trigger = {
		IRE_has_michael_collins = no
		IRE_has_monarchy = no
		has_country_flag = IRE_1937_elections
		has_country_flag = IRE_1942_Election_Held
		NOT = {	has_country_flag = IRE_1947_Election_Held }
		
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

			text = {

		name = ire.170.a

	}

		text = ire.208.d.syndie

		}
	}

		name = ire.208.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = "Ireland sends two divisions to support us."

			division_template = {
				name = "Irish Volunteers"
				division_names_group = USA_GAR_01
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					militia = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				prioritize = { 361 358 360 }
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"1st Dublin Volunteers\" division_template = \"Irish Volunteers\" start_experience_factor = 0.1"
					owner = ROOT
				}

### W.B. Yeats Death ###

country_event = {
	id = ire.57
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.57" }
	title = ire.57.t
	desc = ire.57.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_yeats

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ire.57.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_hog_pau
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Eoin_O'Duffy_hog_pau
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_hog_pau
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Ned_Cronin_hog_pau
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_Kevin_O'Higgins_for_ade
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_Kathleen_Browne_for_pau
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				AND = {
					has_government = national_populist
					has_country_leader_ideology = integralism_subtype
				}
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_Osmond_Esmonde_for_npo
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				AND = {
					has_government = national_populist
					NOT = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = integralism_subtype
					}
				}
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_James_J_Walsh_for_npo
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.02
		}
		
	}
}

			limit = { has_idea = IRE_CATHOLIC }
			remove_ideas = IRE_CATHOLIC
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_acs_religion_labour
		modify_country_flag = {
			flag = IRE_acs_labour
			value = 1
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}

				current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_authdem_pop = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				value = current_IRE_authdem_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_AUTH
		add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
	}
	
	option = { #nah
		name = ire.2511.b
		add_stability = 0.02
	}

country_event = { #The Strange King
	id = ire.331
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.331" }
	title = ire.331.t
	desc = ire.331.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_trench
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.331.a
		
	}	
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.331.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_FF_Natpop
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = national_populist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = national_populist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_IRE_natpop_pop = party_popularity@national_populist
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
					value = current_IRE_natpop_pop
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = national_populist
					popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				}
				set_party_name = {
					name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party
					long_name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
					ideology = national_populist
				}
			}
			set_country_leader_ideology = occultism_subtype
		}
		add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_NATPOP
	}	
	
}

country_event = { #The All Pan-Celtic congress
	id = ire.339
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.339" }
	title = ire.339.t
	desc = ire.339.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_pan_celtic
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_government = national_populist
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader_ideology = integralism_subtype
						has_country_leader_ideology = occultism_subtype
						has_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_larp
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.339.a
		#Isolation
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = IRE_isolation
				}
			}
			add_ideas = IRE_isolation
		}
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.339.b
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_CELT
		set_country_flag = IRE_celtic_union_megaflag
		add_state_core = 983
		add_state_core = 14
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = 983.owner
			   type = annex_everything
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = 14.owner
			   type = annex_everything
			}	
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = ire.339.c
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_CELT2
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ICE
					is_core_of = POR
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		add_state_core = 983
		add_state_core = 14
		add_state_core = 171
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = ICE
			   type = annex_everything
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = POR
			   type = annex_everything
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = 983.owner
			   type = annex_everything
			}
		create_wargoal = {
			   target = 14.owner
			   type = annex_everything
			}	
	}
	
	
}

country_event = { #Fate of the Opressors
	id = ire.345
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.343" }
	title = ire.345.t
	desc = ire.345.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_london
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = IRE
		OR = {
			owns_state = 126
			GBP = {
				owns_state = 126
				is_subject_of = IRE
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_larp
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			every_state = {
			limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_owned_by = IRE
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SCT
							is_core_of = WAL
							is_core_of = IRE
						}
					}
			}
			GBP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			puppet = GBP
		}
		GBP = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GBP_ENG_REPUBLIC
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = GBP_independent_GER
			}
		}
		}
	}	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.b
			trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_larp
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			every_state = {
			limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_owned_by = IRE
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SCT
							is_core_of = WAL
							is_core_of = IRE
						}
					}
			}
			add_core_of = GBP
			GBP = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			puppet = GBP
		}
		GBP = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GBP_FREESTATE
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			}
			create_country_leader = {
			name = "Executive Council"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_English_Exe_Council.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = junta_subtype
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = GBP_independent_GER
			}
		}
		}
		
	}
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.c
		add_timed_idea = { idea = IRE_BRTISHARMY days = 800 } 
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ENG
			}
			add_core_of = IRE
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GBP = {
					is_subject_of = IRE
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
			target = GBP
			transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire.341
				days = 35
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_larp
				}
				set_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_did_it
				country_event = {
					id = ire_monarch.18
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.345.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = IRE_mcdonnell_larp
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		country_event=  {
				id = ire.365
				days = 15
			}
	}			
}

country_event = { #French said yes to peace
	id = ire.354
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire.343" }
	title = ire.354.t
	desc = ire.354.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_no_english
	

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #sure
		name = ire.354.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ENG
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_core_of = WAL
					is_core_of = SCT
					is_core_of = IRE
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			annex_country = {
			target = ENG
			transfer_troops = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SCT = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SCT
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				WAL = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			IRE = {
				annex_country = {
					target = WAL
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = IRE
				OR = {
					tag = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			white_peace = IRE
		}	
	}								
}

		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ire.2605 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ire.2604 option ire.2604.e"
		name = ire.2604.e		# Recognise some religions in particular
		
		add_political_power = -25
		reduce_unionist_tensions = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ire.2605 days = 5 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ire.2604 option ire.2604.f"
		name = ire.2604.f		# State Catholicism
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				has_government = national_populist
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.025
			}
		}
		increase_unionist_tensions = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = ire.2605 days = 5 } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Valera Debates Restoring the Monarchy
	id = ire_monarch.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ire_monarch.1" }
	title = ire_monarch.1.t
	desc = ire_monarch.1.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_crown
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { is_subject = no }

	option = { # Prepare for the Restoration
		name = ire_monarch.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = IRE_future
					option = IRE_FUTURE_DEMOCRACY_SOCCON
				}
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_regency
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Irish Regency Council"
			desc = "POLITICS_IRISH_REGENCY_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/IRE/Portrait_Ireland_Regency_Council.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = christian_democracy_subtype
		}
		set_country_flag = IRE_taoiseach_is_leader

					id = ire_monarch.19
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Integralism
		name = ire_monarch.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25 
			modifier = {
				factor = 75
				has_country_flag = IRE_King_Hugo
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = IRE_monarch
						option = IRE_FUNNY_OBREIN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = IRE_FF_Natpop
		hidden_effect = {

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_soccon_pop = party_popularity@social_conservative
			}
			set_variable = {
				current_IRE_natpop_pop = party_popularity@national_populist
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = current_IRE_soccon_pop
				value = current_IRE_natpop_pop
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = current_IRE_soccon_pop
			}
			set_party_name = {
				name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party
				long_name = IRE_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
				ideology = national_populist
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ire_monarch.11
				days = 22
			}
		}
		add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
		set_country_flag = IRE_FF_NATPOP
	}

			factor = 75

	title = irelandflavour.3914.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		text = irelandflavour.3914.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
		text = irelandflavour.3914.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_government = national_populist }
		text = irelandflavour.3914.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = irelandflavour.3914.d4
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_guinness
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.3914 option irelandflavour.3914.a"
		trigger = { has_democratic_government = yes }
		name = irelandflavour.3914.a
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.3914 option irelandflavour.3914.b"
		trigger = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
		name = irelandflavour.3914.b
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.3914 option irelandflavour.3914.c"
		trigger = { has_government = national_populist }
		name = irelandflavour.3914.c
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.3914 option irelandflavour.3914.e"
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		name = irelandflavour.3914.e
		add_political_power = 10
	}
}

country_event = {  # Death of Joyce
	id = irelandflavour.411
	title = irelandflavour.411.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = no }
		text = irelandflavour.411.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_socialist_government = yes }
		text = irelandflavour.411.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_joyce
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.411 option irelandflavour.411.a"
		name = irelandflavour.411.a
		add_stability = -0.02
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_hog_rso
				has_government = totalist
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Jim_Larkin_Jr_hog_tot
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_hog_rso
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Irish_Congress_of_Trade_Unions_hog_syn
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_hog_rso
				has_government = radical_socialist
				NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_Reconstituted_Labour_Exists }
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Peadar_O'Donnell_hog_rso
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_hog_rso
				has_government = radical_socialist
				has_country_flag = IRE_Reconstituted_Labour_Exists
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_William_X_O'Brien_hog_sde
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_hog_rso
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = taoiseach
			add_ideas = IRE_Thomas_Johnson_hog_sde
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_James_Joyce_for_rso
				has_government = totalist
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_Benjamin_Farrington_for_tot
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_John_O'Leary_for_syn
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_James_Everett_for_sde
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = IRE_William_Butler_Yeats_for_pau
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = foreign_minister
			add_ideas = IRE_Sean_MacBride_for_sde
		}
	}
}

country_event = {  # Dev's birthday cake. 14/10/42
	id = irelandflavour.421
	title = irelandflavour.421.t

	desc = {
		trigger = { has_government = social_conservative }
		text = irelandflavour.421.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { has_government = social_conservative }
			has_war = yes
		}
		text = irelandflavour.421.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			has_war = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_lemass_leads_ff }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = IRE_coalition_with_valera }
		}
		text = irelandflavour.421.d3
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
			has_country_flag = IRE_coalition_with_valera
		}
		text = irelandflavour.421.d4
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_IRE_dev_cake
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { 
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = IRE_VALERA_GONE
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_target = token:social_conservative }
		has_coalition_with_target = yes
		owns_state = 119
		is_subject = no
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.421 option irelandflavour.421.a"
		name = irelandflavour.421.a
		add_political_power = 5
	}
}

country_event = {  # 1916 hidden event (donotlog)
	id = irelandflavour.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = irelandflavour.0 days = 365 }
	}

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }
			country_event = irelandflavour.2
			clr_country_flag = IRE_spindler_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
			country_event = irelandflavour.3
			clr_country_flag = IRE_1916_entente_event
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			country_event = irelandflavour.4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = national_populist }
			country_event = irelandflavour.5
		}
		else = { country_event = irelandflavour.1 }
	}
}

country_event = {  # George is dead
	id = irelandflavour.200
	title = irelandflavour.200.t
	desc = irelandflavour.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_death_george
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		IRE_has_michael_collins = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.200 option irelandflavour.200.a"
		name = irelandflavour.200.a  # Not our concern
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = 10
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.200 option irelandflavour.200.b"
		name = irelandflavour.200.b  # Send a private telegram
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		add_political_power = -5
		CAN = { country_event = { id = irelandflavour.300 days = 2 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event irelandflavour.200 option irelandflavour.200.c"
		name = irelandflavour.200.c  # Give a speech
		ai_chance = { base = 30 }
		add_political_power = -20
		country_event = { id = irelandflavour.500 days = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			CAN = {
				set_country_flag = { flag = IRE_gave_speech days = 30 value = 1 }
				country_event = { id = irelandflavour.300 days = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
}
